--

CREATE TABLE users (
    user_id integer NOT NULL,
    login character varying(80),
    titles character varying(32),
    first_name character varying(256) NOT NULL,
    last_name character varying(256) NOT NULL,
    middle_name character varying(256),
    email character varying(512) NOT NULL,
    gender character varying(1),
    date_of_birth date,
    birth_country character varying(2),
    birth_nationality character varying(2),
    current_nationality character varying(2),
    uri character varying(120),
    date_of_death date,
    type_of_id character varying(1),
    national_id character varying(32),
    password character varying(36),
    salt character varying(24),
    description text,
    image bytea,
    active_p character varying(1),
    receive_notification boolean,
    language character varying(5) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT users_active_p_check CHECK (((active_p)::text = ANY ((ARRAY['A'::character varying, 'I'::character varying, 'D'::character varying])::text[]))),
    CONSTRAINT users_gender_check CHECK (((gender)::text = ANY ((ARRAY['M'::character varying, 'F'::character varying])::text[])))
);
